Program of the Grand Maneuvers of the Japanese Army Stationed in Hebei, First Held After the Expansion of the Japanese Army, Peiping, Tientsin, and Tongzhou Are the Exercise Areas, After the Maneuvers, There Will Be a Military Parade and Encampment in Western Peiping 77

Peiping dispatch: The autumn maneuvers of the Japanese army stationed in North China are being held for the first time since the expansion of the army. The troops participating in this exercise are mainly the 1st Regiment in Tientsin and the 2nd Regiment in Peiping, and will also mobilize garrison troops along the Beining Railway and all special forces. As for the exercise area, it has been decided to be in the wide area of Tientsin, Peiping, Tongzhou, and other areas. Individual joint exercises will be started in Peiping and Tientsin first, then the Tientsin team will gradually expand the scope, while the suburbs of Peiping will hold regimental confrontation exercises under the command of Brigade Commander Kawabe. The final military exercise will be the general command in Tongzhou, under the command of Commander Tadashi, with attack and defense exercises held between Tongzhou and Peiping, ending this grand exercise with the dawn battle on November 4. On the same day, a military parade of all the troops participating in the exercise will be held near Babaoshan outside Xizhimen. At this point, the grand autumn exercise of the Japanese garrison army in North China will come to an end. It is scheduled that on November 5, the troops will return to their respective garrison areas. The exercise schedule is listed below: (1) Joint exercise of regimental infantry (October 26 to 28). The 1st Infantry Regiment will exercise near Peiping, and the 2nd Infantry Regiment will exercise with special forces near Tientsin. (2) Regimental confrontation exercise (from October 30 to November 1): conducted under the command of the Brigade Commander, the 1st and 2nd Infantry Regiments will conduct confrontation exercises near Peiping. (November 2) Gather in Tongzhou, with the general command set in Tongzhou. (3) Conduct a military exercise (from November 3 to 4): conducted under the command of the Army Commander, the exercise will be conducted from Tongzhou to Peiping. (4) Military parade: The military parade will be held near Babaoshan on the 4th, and the troops will encamp in the western suburbs of Peiping. On November 5, the troops will return to their respective garrison areas.

Fu Zuoyi Pays Attention to Ping-Sui Railway Traffic; Enemy Planes Fly to Sui East for Reconnaissance; De Wang Gives a Speech at Jiabu Temple Again 78

Shangdu Correspondence: The bandit army Wang Ying, Li Shouxin, etc., entrenched in Chabei, have been making loud noises about invading the west recently, but they have not yet realized it. According to people who understand the inside story of the bandit army, the reason for the delay is that on the one hand, the defense of Sui Province Chairman Fu Zuoyi is strict, and on the other hand, the internal situation of the bandits is complicated, making it difficult to fight. However, judging from the current situation, the occurrence of war is probably unavoidable. At 7:00 a.m. on the 18th, three enemy planes circled over Shangdu. Judging from their direction, they flew from Dolun. They hovered in the air for a week, then flew southwest to the Sui East area for reconnaissance. After 8:00 a.m., the three planes flew back together. When passing over Shangdu, they did not circle and flew east towards Dolun.

Under the environment of enemy and puppet coveting and invading the Sui East area, Sui Province Chairman Fu Zuoyi, in addition to doing his best to consolidate the defense to prepare for emergencies, pays special attention to the traffic on the Ping-Sui Railway. It is said that Fu Zuoyi issued a notice to all counties along the Ping-Sui Railway a few days ago, roughly stating that the Ping-Sui Railway is a key transportation artery in the northwest, which is related to national defense. In order to prevent bandits from destroying the traffic, special regulations are made for the protection and inspection of bridges and culverts of all sizes within the territory of each county in the Sui Province along the Ping-Sui Railway, and the number of bridges and culverts in each county is detailed, listed and distributed to each county for strict compliance. The local authorities of each county are responsible for assigning security teams or township guides along the road to closely monitor day and night, prohibiting pedestrians from approaching or staying on the road, so as to prevent the bandits from taking the opportunity to destroy it. If the tracks and bridges are destroyed by bandits within the territory of the county after the issuance of this notice, only the county magistrate of the county will be held accountable.

According to people from Jiabu Temple, De Wang summoned a speech at Jiabu Temple the other day, but outsiders have no way of knowing the content. Also, the Mongolian Living Buddha Dongwu Jumuqin Buddha went to Zhangjiakou the other day and stayed there. It is said that he has decided to take the Ping-Sui express train to Ping on the evening of the 18th. After visiting the leaders of Pingfang, he will go south to Jinjing (October 18th).

Guangxi Army Demobilization Completed; Regular Army Still Organized into Two Armies and Six Divisions; Actively Training Militias During Agricultural Leisure 79

Wuzhou Correspondence: Since the realization of peace in Guangxi Province, the army has been completely demobilized, and the people's troops have also returned to their hometowns to serve. The Headquarters of the Guangxi Army is now established in Guilin, but the military designation has not been changed. In addition to the headquarters in Guilin, a headquarters camp has also been established in Nanning. The organization of the headquarters is divided into two offices and twelve departments. The directors and chiefs of the departments have been appointed as follows: Director of the General Office Zheng Chengdian, Director of the Military Affairs Office Lv Jingcun, Chief of the Staff Office Li Xingzhu, Chief of the Military Affairs Office Ge Shixi, Chief of the Adjutant Office Tang Xipu, Chief of the Management Office Xie Zanying, Chief of the Medical Office Xie Sai, Chief of the Political Training Office Pan Yizhi, Chief of the Military Law Office Zhang Jundu, Chief of the Ordnance Office Chen Hanwu, Chief of the Transportation Office Lan Tengjiao, Chief of the Training Office Zhang Zhuangsheng, Chief of the Secretariat Zhu Foding, Chief of the Regiment Affairs Office Li Zuoli. The regular army of the province is organized into two armies and seven divisions, including the 7th Army, with Commander Liao Lei and Deputy Commander Zhou Zujian, under the jurisdiction of the 19th Division Xu Qiming, the 21st Division Yang Junchang, and the 24th Division Cheng Shufen, a total of three divisions; the 15th Army, with Commander Xia Wei and Deputy Commander Zhang Yunsong, under the jurisdiction of the 43rd Division He Weizhen, the 44th Division Wang Zanbin, and the 45th Division Mo Shujie, a total of three divisions, totaling two armies and six divisions. In addition, there is the newly編 First Division under the command of Weng Zhaoyuan.

After the demobilization of the militias and reserve units in Guangxi Province, the training is still being intensified. The militia command headquarters in each district remains the same, only the Yulin Militia Command District is added to command the militias in Yulin. The militia command headquarters is directly under the General Headquarters. There are currently nine militia districts, each with a militia commander and a deputy commander. Most of the militia commanders in each district still hold their posts. The names of the militia commanders in each district are as follows: Nanning District Liang Hansong, Guilin District Chen En Yuan, Wuzhou District Huang Heling, Xunzhou District Chen Liangzuo, Liuzhou District Huang Mian, Pingle District Zhong Zupei, Baise District Su Xinmin, Tianbao District Gao Yangru, Longzhou District Jiang Ruquan. All of the above are major general or lieutenant general ranks. The militia commanders are under the command of the General Headquarters and the supervision of the Provincial Government. Each militia district governs ten or more counties. Each county has a militia command headquarters, with a militia commander concurrently held by the county magistrate and deputy county magistrate. Below the county is a district, with a district joint team headquarters, with a joint team captain concurrently held by the township/district chief. Below the district is a township (town), with a brigade headquarters, with a brigade commander concurrently held by the township chief. Below the township is a village (street), with a reserve team in each village, and the team leader concurrently held by the village chief or street chief. Recently, autumn is ending and winter is coming, and the rice harvest has been completed. The authorities are taking advantage of the agricultural leisure to recruit strong men from various townships into the army for three months of military training. The enlistment will begin in early November, and the method of recruiting strong men will be handled as usual (October 20th).

Fujian-Sui Headquarters Moves to Jian'ou; Zhangsha Welcomes Jiang Dingwen; Jiang Expresses Sincere Words to the People of Fujian; Sui Headquarters Personnel Leave Zhangzhou in Two Batches 80

Xiamen Correspondence: The Pacification Headquarters in Fujian, under the order of the Military Commission, moved from Zhangzhou to Jian'ou in northern Fujian. Pacification Director Jiang Dingwen entered Fujian during the suppression of the rebellion. After the suppression of the Communist bandits, he stationed in Zhangzhou for three years. Now that he is about to move, all sectors of Zhangzhou and Xiamen specially held meetings to bid farewell. Jiang came to Xiamen from Zhangzhou on the 15th. On the 16th, all sectors of Xiamen's party, government, military, business, industry, and academia held a public banquet for Jiang at the Municipal Government. During the banquet, Party Affairs Commissioner Chen Lianfen delivered a farewell speech, followed by Jiang's reply, which roughly stated: "I was ordered to come to Fujian on November 20th, 1933, and three years have passed in a flash. During this period, I suppressed the rebellion and suppressed the Communist bandits. Thanks to the central government's prestige and the soldiers' efforts, and the assistance of the people, we gradually achieved peace. It is not something I dare to take credit for. In November 1934, I was ordered to pacify Fujian, and it has been almost two years since then. I feel sorry that I have not yet completed it. Southern Fujian, especially Xiamen, has a special environment and complex situation. It is particularly difficult to deal with. We should overcome all difficulties, work together, and move towards the road of national revival together. Then the future is bright and we can wait and see. Secondly, when the Chang bandit area was recovered, the Department of Education held special education to transform the people in the bandit area. I think this special education should be expanded and implemented in the coastal areas of southern Fujian to enhance the national consciousness of the people in the coastal areas so that they will not forget their original face. I am ordered to move to Jian'ou, and I will start my journey in the next few days. If I take the waterway, I will first go to Fuzhou, then to Yanping. If I follow the land route, I will first go to Longyan, then to Liancheng Yong'an and then to Yanping to Jian'ou."

On the morning of the 19th, Jiang returned to Zhangzhou from Xiamen. At 3 p.m., all sectors of Zhangzhou also held a farewell meeting at the Lianhuan Society. During the banquet, Jiang gave a reply, stating: "(1) In the three years since I entered Fujian, the first year was the period of suppressing the rebellion and suppressing the bandits, and the second and third years were the period of pacification. Most of the large bandits have been defeated. Now there are still a few scattered bandits. Because the army is often transferred, they have not been completely eliminated, which is regrettable for the suffering of the people. (2) I hope that intellectuals and local gentry and business leaders in Zhangzhou can set an example, take responsibility, and create a path for the country and the nation."

As for the relocation of the Pacification Headquarters, Chief of Staff Li Jianai has led the advance team to Jian'ou last week to make arrangements. The personnel and supplies of each department, the first batch of more than 120 people and files, will take the Wuyang Wheel to Fuzhou from Xiamen on the 22nd, and then go to Jian'ou. The second batch will be completely evacuated from Zhangzhou by the end of the month. The Sui Headquarters will also cease operations in Zhangzhou on the 28th. At the end of last month, the Special Supervisors sent to western Fujian and Zhangzhou and Quanzhou will also return to Zhangzhou before the 25th. Jiang will take the Fuquan Zhang bus to the province from Zhangzhou on the morning of the 21st, and will stay for a short time before transferring to Jian'ou (October 21st).

Yangcheng Lake Crabs Also Have a Good Harvest 84

The famous autumn products of Wu County, Yangcheng Lake crabs, are produced in Xiangcheng District and Weiting District. The annual output is about 2,000 dans, mainly sold to Shanghai, Nanjing, and Suzhou. This autumn, the output of Yangcheng crabs is particularly high. According to the more than 200 fishing boats in Yangcheng Lake that specialize in catching lake crabs, this year's harvest can reach at least 3,000 dans. Currently, the market price of large-sized lake crabs in the production area is 40 yuan per dan, and the secondary grade is 35 to 30 yuan.

Kunshan Malignant Malaria Epidemic 85

Since the beginning of autumn, the weather here has been abnormal, causing malignant malaria to easily spread. Although it has been found in the urban area, the number is still small. However, in rural areas such as Zhengyi, Bacheng, Pengmin, and Yangxiangjing, the surrounding villages have spread severely and are difficult to prevent. Deaths due to this are often heard, and the situation is serious. Currently, in order to seek treatment, the local authorities have organized a mobile malaria eradication team from the County Hospital, which will set off immediately to carry out its work.

Wuxi Yarn and Cloth Prices Soar Endlessly 86

The market price of cotton yarn in the county is soaring. Because the factory's current yarn is scarce, there is a situation of supply falling short of demand. On the 20th, the market price of each brand soared by 10 to 12 yuan. Various yarn shops think highly of the price and are still unwilling to sell the existing goods. The reasons are: (1) The sales of cotton cloth are more prosperous than in the past. In Shanghai, because the currency system of Guangdong and Guangxi has been unified with the central government, the cotton cloth trade in these two provinces is ordering in large quantities from Shanghai, resulting in a large decrease in cotton cloth; (2) After improvement, Chinese cotton is almost the same as American cotton, but the price is lower than American cotton. Therefore, Japanese merchants, in addition to buying as much cotton as possible in North China, are also ordering it in Shanghai and other places, resulting in Chinese yarn factories lacking raw materials, while sales are very active. Therefore, under this situation, the price of cotton yarn cannot be stopped, breaking the record of more than ten years. Compared with the lowest time in the local yarn market, it has risen by nearly 40 yuan per piece. The market price is still continuing to rise; (3) The price of yarn has also soared, and the price of cotton textiles has also risen accordingly. The original price of 16-pound coarse cloth produced by local factories such as Qingfeng, Gengyu, and Shenxin was 9 yuan per piece, but recently it has risen to 11 yuan, and there is no stock available for sale. The price of mercerized money cloth in various city markets has also soared, rising by 3 to 5 cents per yard. All the stocks of various cloth factories have been collected by various silk shops. Yesterday, the price of Shuangyu Gengyu coarse cloth broke the 12 yuan mark.

Rice Market Prices Remain Firm 87

Wuxi has always been a gathering area for rice. Anhui Province is a rice-producing area. Therefore, whenever the new grains are harvested, general merchants transport rice to Wuxi for sale. The opening price is usually lower, but although the goods in various rice shops are pouring in, the market price remains firm. Qingbai japonica rice is 9 yuan and 1 jiao per stone. According to people in the industry, the reasons for the firm rice market this time are: Although this autumn harvest is better than last year, and the goods arriving are also more than in previous years, there are fewer rice merchants from Anhui Province selling in Wuxi than last year. This is because a certain party recently sent Chinese businessmen to purchase large quantities of rice in the Su-Wan area, load them onto sea vessels, and transport them to a certain country. Therefore, the market price in Wuxi is unlikely to fall in the near future.

Special Goods Oversupplied 88

The local opium houses, opium dens, and opium smoking places that previously received the second annual business license have now expired. Now that the third annual session has begun, they have all submitted a report to the county government requesting to continue their business. After County Magistrate Long approved the opium houses Dachang, Yongxing, Futai, Jiatian, the opium dens Yitai, Dalong, Yuanji, Dasheng, Yonghe, Qiuguang, Yongda, Xinxing, Yunji, Xiexin, Shengli, Youli, Xiecheng, and thirteen others, and the opium smoking places Luo Hongchang, Shenchang, Yongyu, Zhenxin, and fifty-seven others, they submitted a report to the Department of Civil Affairs for review yesterday. Also, the local official soil market price has gradually soared. Yuntu has risen by 2 jiao and 4 fen per liang. The original price was 1 yuan and 7 jiao, but now it costs 2 yuan and 9 jiao and 4 fen. Moreover, various opium houses and shops have very few sources, and there is a danger of running out of stock due to oversupply. Smokers throughout the county are in a state of panic.

Yangzhou Director Jian of the Department Arrives in Yangzhou for Inspection 89

Wanfu Bridge in the east of this county is a necessary passage for transportation in Yangzhou, Taizhou and other places. Since it was destroyed by Sun Jun in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the bridge has been a large project and it is not easy to repair. Although local people have been running around to raise funds for repairs, it has been difficult to work due to the difficulty of fundraising. Later, the National Economic Council and the Jiangsu Provincial Government allocated funds for repairs, which started this spring. After several months, the work was often stopped due to insufficient funds and materials, which made it difficult for the bridge to be completed. It is now known that Shen Baixian, Director of the Department of Construction, came to Yangzhou from the province on the morning of the 21st with technical personnel to inspect the actual situation of the project and complete the bridge as soon as possible, and then went to Wanfu Bridge for inspection.

Truth About Bai Shulan Robbery Case 90

Regarding the case of the robbery of Wang Yuanzhang, a clerk of the Jiangsu Bank, who was robbed of ten yuan of remittances from a Zhou family in Dongguan Street in the old city of Jiangdu, the county government, according to the report of accountant Jiang Yingbo and the oral statements of Wang Yuanzhang, immediately ordered the Public Security Investigation Team and the Third Sub-station in charge to arrest and investigate the robbers. Now, Hu Yaozhen, the detective of the team, has learned the truth. Wang Yuanzhang is addicted to gambling. When passing through Five Lane, he saw a gambling table and participated in gambling, losing eight yuan. He used the ten yuan bill for remittance to find two yuan back (both red Jiaotong Bank bills). Later, Wang felt cheated and argued with the stall owner, intending to reclaim it. Seeing that the situation was not good, the stall owners fled together. Jiang witnessed this. When Wang chased after Jiang, he embellished the report that he had been robbed. Yesterday (19th), the detective led detectives Cui Xingwu and arrested a gambler named Cao Wanyuan at the west entrance of Duomai Lane. He confessed the same as before and summoned Wang Yuanzhang to the team to confront him. It is said that both sides have requested to be exempted from further investigation, and Cao compensated Wang for his losses. The original was detained by the team, waiting for further interrogation.

Nantong Recruiting Doctors to Treat the Epidemic 91

The epidemic in Tongyi has recently spread to a wider area. In addition to recruiting more than 60 doctors from various hospitals and health agencies to depart for diagnosis and treatment, the Epidemic Prevention Association is also sending a large number of medical personnel to Nantong to prevent and control the epidemic. Danyang Monster Found in Fish Pond 92

In the daming river pond in Xujiawei, east of Yaojia Bridge in this county, it is said that there is a very fierce water ghost. After nightfall, the villagers warned each other not to walk past it. Those who mistakenly walked near it would be fascinated and drown without realizing it. A villager named Zhang, a local rich man, refuted the idea of ghosts and gods. One night, he secretly carried a pistol and walked alone along the shore. Before long, he felt that his movements were slightly restricted, as if he was being pulled by something in the dark. He felt a little timid, but then he regained his spirit and moved forward bravely. Suddenly, he saw an object lying in the pond, shaped like a giant tortoise, raising its head outwards, frequently sucking in its breath, as if using it to pull pedestrians into the pond. Zhang knew that the so-called haunting of the water ghost must be this thing. He quickly raised his gun and shot it from a distance, and there was a sound of falling into the water. The next morning, he told the villagers what he had seen. The villagers drained the fish pond and searched for it. They found an object, its body as soft as cotton, less than a foot long, unlike the giant tortoise seen last night, but one of its feet was injured, obviously a gunshot wound. So they captured it and placed it in a large tank in the ancestral hall, filled with water. The monster swelled up, and the tank could not hold it, and it even burst. When the water was drained, it shrank back to its original shape. As for what it is, there is no way to name it. Therefore, it is recorded for the study of naturalists.

Jiaxing Establishment of Collection Sub-Counter 93

In order to reorganize the income of land taxes and eliminate long-standing malpractices, the Jiaxing County Government has set up land registration officers to collect land taxes and abolish tax collection officials. It is now planning to set up collection sub-counters in the urban area, Xinfeng, Xinzhen, Wangdian, Wangjiangjing and other places. All the personnel have been allocated and will be announced soon. The office buildings of each sub-counter are currently being sought and repaired. Each sub-counter will be established in early November, with a temporary period of three months to facilitate local payments by grain households. As for households with outstanding taxes, they are now being transferred and urged by the Tax Collection Office, so the number of collections has gradually improved recently.

Hangzhou Postponement of Literature Exhibition 94

The Zhejiang Literature Exhibition hosted by the Zhejiang Provincial Library has been decided by the design committee at a standing committee meeting due to the approaching exhibition period: (1) The exhibition date will be changed to November 1st and will close on the 15th; (2) The exhibition venue will be decided at the Provincial Library on Daxue Road, but a part of the rubbings will be displayed at the Gushan Branch. The Zhejiang provincial product collection sub-committees have mostly shipped cultural relics to Hangzhou. In the Ning district, in addition to a few counties such as Cixiao sending them by post, they still need to wait for the Tianyi Pavilion to transport books before sending them together. A lot of precious books were collected in the Wen district, and they have been transferred to Hangzhou via Shanghai, totaling 17 large wooden boxes and more than 560 pieces of cultural relics, and the registration and editing have begun.

Sanjiang Lock Siltation Reorganization 95

The Qianjiang Shaoxing Duantang Lock Project Office believes that since the beginning of autumn, the weather has been dry and Cao'e River has a small flow and low water level. Now it is dry to 5.63 meters, while the autumn tide in the outer port is surging and the mud and sand are swelling with the tide, reaching 6.05 meters, exceeding the inland river water level by 0.42 meters. The river flow is far away from the Sanjiang Lock, resulting in a lock port of more than ten miles long. After the Wang Fan tide in August of the lunar calendar, the lock port was completely silted up, and a special report was submitted to the Department of Construction. The provincial government plans to make fundamental improvements, which must wait for the completion of the river mouth plan and the determination of the river bank line before starting. The current relief method should be to temporarily hire workers to excavate, then release water for flushing, and when the silted sand increases to 5 centimeters above the inland river surface, one or two holes should be opened for flushing. The project office has been ordered to investigate the actual situation and apply it as appropriate.

Ningbo Hengfeng Factory Debt Dispute 96

Hengfeng Cloth Factory in Ningbo owed Dayuanzhuang 33,900 yuan in national currency and Ruifengzhuang more than 5,200 yuan. The two sides had a dispute and were involved in litigation at the Zheng County Local Court. The local court then ruled that the debt should be repaid in six equal installments within six months. Hengfeng refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court, which scheduled a hearing on the 24th of this month. The two villages, Dayuan and Ruifeng, operate on the basis of deposits and loans from money houses. If the debt can be repaid in installments and the deposits can be withdrawn at any time, the operation of the money house will be in danger. Moreover, Hengfeng Factory has ample assets and the shareholders are very wealthy. Whether it is the partnership property or the shareholders' capital, it is possible to pay off the debt in one lump sum. Te Xing asked the Money Industry Association to transfer a letter to the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce, which was sent to the party and government organs for detailed explanation, and transferred a letter to the Third Branch of the Zhejiang Higher Court for investigation, requesting to amend the judgment to repay in one lump sum in order to maintain the money industry.

Over a Thousand Athletes Compete in the City Center, City Games Open Today. Opening Ceremony at 9 AM, Mayor Attends to Give Speech. Today Features Group Performances and a Drill Display by Three Thousand Students. Referees Will Assemble and Depart from Various Locations at 8 AM. 97

The long-awaited Fourth Municipal Games of this city are scheduled to open today. The games will last for three days at the Municipal Central Sports Field. The opening ceremony will be held at 9 AM today. Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and others will attend to deliver speeches. No tickets will be sold for the event; the public is welcome to attend freely. Details are as follows:

Arrangements at the Venue

The venue arrangements have been completed, and the track and field have been newly renovated. The guest seating is located on the west platform, accessible by invitation only. Stands No. 1, 4, and 6 are for athletes, while stands No. 3, 5, 7, 8, 9, 10, and 11 are for the public and are free of charge. The remaining stands are for students from various schools, with access from the east platform. Loudspeakers have been installed throughout the venue.

Jingwu Physical Culture Association Expands Membership Recruitment 100

The Jingwu Physical Culture Association of this city is the earliest organization in the country to promote martial arts. Over the past 20 years, it has produced numerous talents, and its branches are numerous. Its three-star banner has reached as far as the Nanyang Islands. There are three branches in Shanghai, one on North Sichuan Road, one at the Continental Emporium on Nanjing Road, and one on Rue Lubei. The internal facilities focus on social education and are highly trusted by people from all walks of life. Recently, it has stepped up its internal work: (1) Expanding membership recruitment. This recruitment is divided into two types: (1) Ordinary members, who enjoy all the benefits of the association and pay an annual fee of 12 yuan. (2) Traveling members, who pay a fee for three years. (2) Strengthening the martial arts department. In addition to the original Tan Tui, Tai Chi, Fanzi, Mantis, and Chaquan styles, which are taught by famous masters such as Zhao Yunhe, Wu Jianquan, Zhao Shouchun, and Chen Guoqing, there will be a martial arts lecture and a performance once a month. For Western boxing, a sparring class has been established, and Chen Hanqiang has been hired as the instructor. Ping Weiren, who recently won a championship in the Nanyang Islands, has also joined the training. (3) Reorganizing the table tennis team. This team is one of the four strongest teams in Shanghai. Last autumn, after defeating the Japanese Rikkyo team, its reputation rose sharply. It has recently been reorganized and intensified training to prepare for participation in various cup competitions. As for the Baihong track and field team, which is hosted by the association, it recently held a sports meet to test the results of senior members. Other activities, such as the first aid class and the singing class, are also actively underway. It is reported that the association will organize a trip to Songjiang Yushan on the 25th of this month, with a round-trip fare of only 2 yuan in national currency.

Wanxia Cup Table Tennis News 104

Since the beginning of the Wanxia Cup, the following teams have registered to join: Wanxia, Wanxia Zhi, Wanxia Ren, Wanxia Yong, and Boyang. The cup competition adopts the "Ten Ping Rules." Each team only pays a competition fee of 1 yuan and a deposit of 2 yuan. The competition venue is rotated among the teams and is absolutely not restricted by region. All table tennis organizations in the city are welcome to register to participate in the competition. The deadline for registration is the 30th of this month. Participating teams are requested to contact the Wanxia Table Tennis Team in Hou Deli, Tangjiawan, Ximen as soon as possible.

Xiguang Cross Country Team, Longhua Long Distance Race, Public Registration Started Yesterday, Scheduled to Start Race on the Morning of the 8th of Next Month 107

The Fourth Longhua Round Trip Long Distance Race organized by the Xiguang Cross Country Team is scheduled to start on the morning of the 8th of next month in front of the Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road, Nanshi. The entire distance is 12 miles long, about 20,000 meters. Registration has started yesterday and is open to the public, regardless of qualifications. Anyone with amateur sports qualifications can register to participate, but please pay attention to the following points: (1) Must be between 17 and 40 years old. (2) When registering, except for Xiguang team members, each person will be charged 15 cents in national currency to show restriction. (5) The registration office is at No. 25 Shanxi Road, Public Concession, the team's office. For remote mail registration, sufficient postage stamps are required. Blank letters are invalid. Also, in view of the fact that the competition has been monopolized by general famous players in Shanghai in previous years, and new entrants are generally disappointed, and the round trip of about 10,000 meters for the whole journey is long and difficult, the team has added more places to emphasize quality and quantity. All 100 selected names will receive souvenirs, and the top performers will receive special awards. Anyone who breaks the team's highest record of 1 minute 3 seconds and 6 seconds will be awarded a large silver cup to encourage them.

Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Faculty and Staff Association Representative Conference Elects New Directors and Discusses Educational and Administrative Issues 110

The 19th Representative Conference of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Faculty and Staff Association was held on October 18th at the Nanjing Provincial Nanjing Girls' High School. Attendees included Liu Mengjin (from Zhenjiang Normal School, also a previous director), Zhang Songnian (from Haizhou Normal School, also a previous director), Wu Zonghan (from Wuxi Normal School, also a previous director), Liu Qinpu (from Loushi Normal School), Jin Rongxuan (from Zhenjiang High School), Chu Jin (from Jiangsu Agricultural School, also a previous director), Gu Dubi (from Yixing Agricultural School), Yang Yafu (from Jiangsu Industrial School), Meng Dacheng (from Songjiang Girls' High School), Zhang Zhongyou (from Luoyang Normal School, also a previous director), Mei Mu (from Huaian Normal School), Huang Zemin (from Nanjing Girls' High School), Ye Shaonong (from Zhenjiang High School), Wang Dagang, Zhong Ziming (from Shanghai High School), Gao Zhihou (from Wusong Fisheries School), Chen Duanben (from Jiangsu Women's Normal School), Wu Ziwo (from Zhenjiang Normal School), Wu Cangsu (previous director), Lü Suizhi (from Yangzhou High School), Zhu Xizi, Chen Zhulun (from Ningbo High School), Sun Yonggang (from Xuzhou High School), Ren Yizun (from Nantong High School), Li Jinlin (from Jiangsu High School), Wu Heling (from Xuzhou Women's Normal School), Zhao Jingyuan (representing Lianyungang Fisheries and Canal Rural Normal School), Zhang Tongmo (previous director, from Rushi Normal School), Zhang Zikun (representing Shihuzhen Rural Normal School), and Mao Peiqing (representing Taizhou Normal School). Liu Jing was present as an observer. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Tongmo, with Liu Mengjin as the recorder. Formalities were observed, an opening address was given, and the association's work was reported. Next, seven articles of the association's charter were amended: (1) Article 4, "Temporary Meeting" was changed to "Temporary Representative Conference;" (2) the following was added after Article 4: "This association shall have one representative to the Provincial Education Funding Committee, elected by the Representative Conference for a term of one semester." Eight, twenty-three votes were cast. Zhang Zhongyou received ten votes, Zhang Tongmo nineteen votes, Liu Mengjin nineteen votes, Wu Han eighteen votes, and Zhang Songping sixteen votes. The above nineteen people were elected as directors. Following, Li Jinlin received thirteen votes, Sun Yonggang twelve votes, and Wu Cangsu eleven votes. The above five people were elected as alternate directors. Nine, the results of the election of the representative to the Provincial Education Funding Committee were as follows: Zhang Tongmo sixteen votes, elected; Huang Zemin three votes. Ten, Zhang Tongmo, having been elected as the representative to the Provincial Education Funding Committee, found it difficult to attend to the duties of a director and requested to resign from the position of director. It was resolved that Zhang Tongmo's resignation from the position of director be approved, and that Li Jinlin, who received the next highest number of votes, should fill the vacancy. Eleven, the duties of the directors were assigned as follows: Standing Committee: Huang Zemin, Zhang Zhongyou, Meng Jin; Secretary: Wu Zonghan; Editor: Zhang Songnian; Research: Li Jinlin; Accountant: Lü Suizhi; Affairs: Wu Heling; Public Relations: Chu Jin. Thirteen, the meeting continued to discuss proposals, with Huang Zemin as chairman and Wu Zonghan as recorder. First, training: (1) In view of the seriousness of the national crisis, what should the association's colleagues express regarding young students? It was resolved that a letter to young students be issued in the name of the association (to be drafted by the Jiangning High School, which originally proposed the motion) and that the executive committee should execute it. (2) (3) (omitted)

(4) Submit a request to the Department of Education to forward a request to the Ministry of Education to increase the number of class hours for music and library science education in senior high school general education programs. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to forward the request to the Ministry of Education, stipulating one hour each per week for music and library science. (5) Some subjects in normal schools lack suitable textbooks. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to forward a request to the Ministry of Education to compile and print them as soon as possible for teaching purposes. (6) It is proposed that the conference send a letter to all provincial schools regarding the "Outline of Special Education for Secondary Schools" promulgated by the Department, requesting them to conduct regional research on the subjects of extracurricular group teaching and to adopt common teaching materials and lectures to promote communication and increase efficiency. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to open training classes to cultivate professors and to send a letter to the schools concerned from this association to facilitate mutual research. (7) The teaching progress of various subjects in the province's normal schools has not been promulgated in many cases. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to quickly stipulate the teaching progress for senior high school general education programs. The teaching progress already promulgated for junior high schools is not applicable and should be revised. (8) The teaching progress of various subjects in senior high school vocational schools has not been promulgated in many cases. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to forward a request to the Ministry of Education to stipulate it as soon as possible for compliance. (9) The equipment for history and geography teaching in provincial secondary schools is largely lacking. It was resolved to request the Department of Education to designate special funds to improve the equipment to facilitate teaching. Second, administration: (10) It was resolved to request the Department of Education to cancel the regional restrictions for normal schools enrolling new students. (11) It was resolved to submit a request to the Department to increase the number of junior high school classes in provincial high schools and to approve the increase in the number of classes in county junior high schools to relieve unemployed youth. (12) It was resolved to submit a request to the Department to approve the exemption of restrictions on normal school graduates returning to serve in their native counties. Third, advanced studies and benefits: (13) It was resolved to submit a request to the Department to promptly announce the implementation measures for teachers who have served in a school for nine years to be entitled to one year of advanced studies. (14) It was resolved to submit a request to the Department of Education to forward a request to the Ministry of Education stipulating that staff members who have served in a school for nine years should receive the same treatment as teachers and be allowed to pursue advanced studies for one year. It was resolved to not only submit the request to the Department of Education for forwarding but also to directly request the Ministry of Education. (15) This association has repeatedly submitted requests to the Department of Education to dispatch staff members from various provincial schools to conduct educational inspections at home and abroad, but this has not been implemented. It was resolved to entrust the executive committee to handle it. (16) It was resolved to present a request to the Department of Education to improve the budget system of secondary schools to make the new salary item flexible to implement the system of full-time teachers. (17) It was resolved to present a request to the Central Government to clearly interpret whether secondary school faculty and staff are civil servants. (18) After faculty and staff of various schools have paid income tax, donations designated by higher authorities should be voluntary. It was resolved to notify the principals of each school and to file the matter with the Department for record. (19) Secondary school faculty and staff who pay income tax in accordance with the regulations for self-employed professionals should deduct the necessary expenses for their work before calculating their taxable income. It was resolved to wait for the Central Government to interpret whether staff members are civil servants before the executive committee decides on measures to handle the matter. (20) It was resolved to present a request to the Department of Education to clearly order that newly appointed principals should not arbitrarily replace faculty and staff to comply with the law. (21) It was resolved to request the Department of Education to use donation funds to increase the salaries of teachers to maintain their livelihood. (22) Provincial inspectors should conduct inspections of secondary schools by specializing in different subjects. (23) It was resolved to request the Department of Education to stipulate objective standards for provincial inspectors as soon as possible. (24) It was suggested that the Department of Education inspectors should consider the opinions of the principals when making evaluations. It was resolved that the executive committee should handle the above three items, taking into account the resolution of item 17. Sixth, other: (25) It was resolved to present a request to the Department of Education to forward a request to the Central Government to clearly order the promulgation of a Teachers' Day to avoid inconsistencies. (26) It was resolved that, in principle, the association's office could be merged with the province's social education agencies and provincial primary schools, and that the executive committee should proceed accordingly. The original preparatory committee should be terminated. (27) It was resolved to entrust the executive committee to handle Zhang Shizai's request to exchange a portion of the base with the association. (28) It was resolved to determine the location of the next conference: first choice, Zhenjiang; second choice, Yangzhou. (29) It was resolved to hold a biology research conference in this session. (30) It was resolved that the executive committee should send a telegram to celebrate the birthday of Chairman Chiang.

Zhejiang Literature Exhibition's Exhibits Substantially Enriched Opening Date Revised to November 1st at Provincial Library Exhibits from Various Regions of Zhejiang and Beijing-Shanghai Arriving in Hangzhou 112

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, in order to promote local literature and advocate scholarship, designated the Provincial Library to organize the Zhejiang Literature Exhibition. A design committee and exhibit collection subcommittees in Beijing-Shanghai and other regions were formed, and preparations have been underway for several months. Previously, the Department of Education had instructed all counties to first organize county literature exhibitions, and then to select the best exhibits to send to Hangzhou. Most counties complied with the order and held exhibitions. After the exhibitions, many sent exhibits to their respective regional subcommittees for compilation. The Provincial Library sent personnel to collect the exhibits, or the exhibits were sent directly from various locations. As of yesterday, exhibits had arrived from Hangzhou County, Tonglu, Yuhang, former Jiaxing, Huzhou, Shaoxing, Jinhua, Quzhou, Cixi, Dinghai, Taishun, and other areas, totaling over 5,500 items. Wenzhou, Yin County, Pinghu, and other areas are either en route or awaiting collection and transport. In Beijing, dozens of rare treasures from private collections have been transported to Nanjing. The Shanghai exhibit collection subcommittee has gathered a collection. The library sent a representative to Beijing on the 16th to make arrangements. It is reported that the Relics Preservation Society, the Institute of History and Philology, and various public and private parties have been supportive and have offered many exhibits. The preparatory work for the exhibition is being carried out by a portion of the Provincial Library's staff as volunteers. Due to the late arrival of exhibits from distant regions and the time required for editing, the original opening date of October 26th was deemed too hasty. After deliberation at the Standing Committee meeting of the Design Committee yesterday (the 19th), the opening date was revised to November 1st and the closing date to November 15th, to allow for continued collection and arrangement. The Standing Committee also resolved several issues related to the grouping and examination of exhibits. It is reported that the exhibits sent by various parties include rare Zhejiang local chronicles, manuscript copies of writings by distinguished figures, calligraphy, rubbings of bronze and stone inscriptions, clothing and items used by local worthies, and relics of Zhejiang revolutionary martyrs. Many of the exhibits collected are valuable. Rare books from the Tianyi Pavilion and Jiaye Library will also be exhibited. At that time, the confluence of various strengths will surely create a magnificent spectacle. The collection work in Shanghai is continuing, and those who are enthusiastic about supporting the effort can contact the Ningbo Road Fuyuan Money Exchange exhibit collection subcommittee.

Great China University Establishes Lectures on Civic Education 119

Great China University has established a series of lectures on civic education this semester, inviting experts from both inside and outside the university to speak during commemoration week. The speakers and topics are as follows: Ou Yuanhuai on the meaning and purpose of civic education; Chu Minyi on the National Assembly and civic education; Zhang Sumin on national economic construction and civic education; Pan Gongzhan on the New Life Movement and civic education; Zou Bingwen on the rural reconstruction movement and civic education; Wu Yunzhai on the movement to promote domestic goods and civic education; Huang Renzhi on civic education in extraordinary times; Yu Qingtang on social education and civic education; Sun Yuanzeng on a comparative view of British and Italian civic education; Wang Yukai on the mission of university students in civic education; and Lu Jizeng on the prospects of civic education in our country. Food prices, especially flour, surged and hit the upper daily limit The forward price has reached 3.9025 yuan, the highest peak since the exchange was founded 120

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed an upward trend again, setting a new record high. Although the quotation of foreign wheat was flat, due to the strong momentum of the traders, it was impossible to speculate based on common sense. As a result, the market price rose and fell sharply. When prices rose, the market was full of bullish sentiment. The opening price immediately rose by one or two cents. Then, the off-market big players frequently traded and bought up the supply. The factory owners in this city and other cities and towns, seeing the difficulty in buying wheat, were silent and allowed the price to rise sharply. As a result, the market soared, and made significant progress. During the day, a total of 700,000 to 800,000 bags of flour were transacted, and the market increased by seven to eight cents. When the market opened in the afternoon, due to the futures wheat market jumping by another corner of a yuan, the market sentiment became even more excited. The opening price for each month rose by a corner of a yuan. Therefore, after the second round of trading, the market was invisibly suspended due to the price limit. This is the highest peak since the establishment of the exchange. The market price in March reached 3.9025 yuan. If there were no daily price limits, it might have reached an alarming record of 4 yuan. It is not known whether the relevant authorities have noticed this.

The price of future wheat has not stopped rising The far-term has soared by a huge 0.256 yuan 121

Yesterday, in the futures wheat market, the prices for all months jumped across the board at the opening, and the degree of increase was unprecedented in recent years. The prices for December and January have increased by a huge 0.256 yuan. This situation is as if there is already a shortage of food, causing speculators to raise prices arbitrarily. At the opening price, the sentiment of off-market investors was good. Although there were many transactions, the prices for each month rose by varying amounts of 0.04 to 0.07 yuan. When the market opened in the afternoon, due to the active participation of the cotton yarn and securities traders, the narrow market was unable to resist the huge forces. As a result, the opening price jumped across the board by 0.123 yuan, and the trading was unprecedented. Since then, the market has been calm for the recent two months, and the far-term has continued to be good. This situation is not related to actual sales and is purely speculative. According to this trend, after the price is raised step by step, it will inevitably approach the pricing of foreign wheat before stopping. Currently, the price of wheat is high, and transactions are not smooth. The price of medium-quality wheat has risen by 0.15 yuan. Fuxin sold 4,000 bags, and Shentai sold 1,000 bags.

Guangdong Traders Purchase High-Quality Unpolished Rice 122

Yesterday, about 10,000 bags of rice arrived, but traders from various regions were even more eager to purchase, especially traders from Guangzhou and Shantou. Traders in this street took the opportunity to purchase. Traders from Guangzhou vigorously searched for unpolished rice, but the supply of unpolished rice in the market was scarce. All of the rice in the hands of hawkers was purchased by traders from Guangzhou. Yesterday, the price was raised to 8.78 yuan to purchase high-quality unpolished rice, but they were still unable to purchase as much as they wanted. Therefore, they only purchased 1,000 to 2,000 bags of unpolished Yangjian, early unpolished machine-milled rice, and rice flour. Traders from Shantou and this street purchased machine-milled rice. The market price immediately soared by 0.23 yuan. If the volume of sales continues to be strong, the market price may rise further. Northern Sales of River Rice Reliant on Sales to Northern Regions 123

(South of Shanghai) Yesterday, more than 30 firms arrived from various sources, with a total of more than 6,000 stones of rice. The color of new Yin Yuan is still fresh.

Sales of various types of rice in the market, such as new japonica rice, Yang Dubu Jian, new Yin Yuan, and green seeds, turned better, while the sales of broken japonica rice and new and old rice remained sluggish. Silk and Tea　American Silk Firm's Silk Sales Are Brisk　Selling Prices Continue to Rise Higher Than Before　More Than 580 Bales Were Traded Yesterday 124

Recently, the gradual reduction in the inventory of raw silk in New York has led to the repeated rise in the silk market between Japan and the United States. As of yesterday, the selling prices of current and forward contracts have risen by an average of about 40 yuan compared to the beginning of this month. The prices of near and far futures in New York have also risen by about seven points. As a result, silk sales in Shanghai this week have become more active. The prices of exported silk are soaring, and the appetite is strong, which is only seen in the past two months. Yesterday, the prices of New York, Shanghai, and Guangdong silk held firm, as factories were in great need and inventories were low, so they rose by another three points. Japanese silk only rose by one or two points. Yokohama spot prices continued to rise by five yuan, and forward prices by a small one yuan. Sales of American silk firm's silk in Shanghai continued to be brisk, and French silk was also satisfactory. Selling prices rose by 30 yuan compared to the beginning of this week. Market sentiment is increasingly optimistic, so silk sales to users also became active yesterday, and the appetite was not weak, making the silk market even more profitable. Yesterday, more than 580 bales of silk were traded in Shanghai, with domestic sales accounting for about one-fifth.

Yarn Flower: Yarn Market Waves Rise and Fall, Differing Bull and Bear Views Cause Sudden Ups and Downs, Highest This Month Reaching 240 Yuan, Unfavorable Afternoon News Causes Slight Decline, Current Yarn Stabilizes Around 6 Yuan 125

Yarn Market: Ups and downs, sudden rises and falls, like a storm. Market sentiment is chaotic and inconsistent, with bulls and bears out of step. In reality, prices have reached a high level, full of twists and turns. However, it is said that a certain major player from the past has already gone long in the November futures, preparing to take delivery. Therefore, buying momentum is strong, and new peaks are frequently reached, rising to 240 yuan this month. It is found that there are still 9,000 bales left in the account. November penetrated 30 yuan outside to 230 yuan. However, on-site yarn sales are sluggish and difficult. Everyone is taking a wait-and-see attitude. Therefore, during the third session in the afternoon, the market became restless, with unfavorable news causing declines in various months. The market rebounded at the close, but remained in chaos for the time being, with frequent trading continuing until late at night. Observing the overall trend, the bulls are holding onto November without letting go. A certain individual is using their skills, dragging in on this number and selling heavily on that number, causing the market price to fluctuate and surge. In short, prices are too high, and once there is a reaction, it will be difficult to stop. One must be cautious.

The November Futures Market is Especially Strong

The labeled yarn market opened with calm. October remained unchanged, November fell by five cents, and distant months rose by 1.13 to 0.20 yuan. March remained unchanged. In the second session, the bullish trend rose again, but the current yarn situation was exceptionally weak, with selling prices flat. It is said that the customer group is actually selling, and the Tianjin group is offering a large number of long positions, so the upward momentum is not strong. Unexpectedly, in the third session, the near-month gains were particularly strong, surpassing the previous day's high. This month was 239.90 yuan, and November was 251 yuan. However, the last two months fell by 0.09 to 1.00 yuan. By the time of closing, the near-month recovered by 0.05 yuan, and the distant month rose by 0.56 yuan. The results for labeled yarn showed near-month prices up 3.50 yuan from the previous day's closing price, and distant-month prices up 2.20 to 1.00 yuan.
